class=\"exmenu\">\n        <a href=\"http://www.saatchigallery.com/selfie/reviews.php\" id=\"review\">Press reviews</a>\n    </div>\n    <div class=\"exdescription\">\n        <div class=\"picholder_l\">\n            <a href=\"http://www.saatchigallery.com/selfie\">\n                <img src=\"/smart-includes/assets/images/selfie.jpg\" alt=\"From Selfie to Self-Expression\">\n            </a>\n        </div>\n        <div class=\"partshowbox_l\">\n            Saatchi Gallery and Huawei&nbsp;have teamed up to present From Selfie to Self-Expression. This is the world’s first exhibition exploring the history of the selfie from the old masters to the present day, and celebrates the truly creative potential of a form of expression often derided for its inanity.\n            <br>\n            <br>\n            The show also highlights the emerging role of the mobile phone as an artistic medium for self-expression by commissioning ten exciting young British photographers to create new works using Huawei’s newest breakthrough dual lens smartphones co-engineered with Leica.\n            <a href=\"http://www.saatchigallery.com/selfie\">Read&nbsp;more</a>\n            <br>\n            <br>\n            <div class=\"exnotice\">\n                <font style=\"font-size: 11px; color:#51585D; font-family: arial,verdana,tahoma,sans-serif; font-weight:bold;\">\n                    <b>Presented by</b>\n                </font>\n                <br>\n                <a href=\"http://consumer.huawei.com/uk/index.htm\" target=\"_blank\">\n                    <img src=\"/smart-includes/assets/images/huawei_logo.jpg\" style=\"margin-top:10px;\">\n                </a>\n            </div>\n\n        </div>\n        <div class=\"clearfix\"></div>\n    </div>\n\n</div><div class=\"splitter\"></div><div class=\"exhibition\">\n    <a href=\"http://www.saatchigallery.com/art/tsuyoshi_maekawa.php\" class=\"underliner\">\n        <h3>SALON 001: TSUYOSHI MAEKAWA</h3>\n    </a>\n    <span class=\"date\">24 February - 14 May 2017</span>\n    <div class=\"exmenu\">\n       <a href=\"http://www.saatchigallery.com/video-tour-tsuyoshi-maekawa.htm\" id=\"video\" target=\"_blank\">Video Tour</a>\n        <a href=\"http://www.saatchigallery.com/art/salon_installation_views.php\" id=\"review\">Installation views</a>\n    </div>\n\n    <div class=\"exdescription\">\n        <div class=\"picholder_l\">\n            <a href=\"http://www.saatchigallery.com/art/tsuyoshi_maekawa.php\">\n                <img src=\"/smart-includes/assets/images/Maekawa_Mannaka.jpg\" alt=\"Tsuyoshi Maekawa\">\n            </a>\n        </div>\n        <div class=\"partshowbox_l\">\n            Saatchi Gallery launches a new exhibition space; SALON.\n            <br>\n            Inaugurated in collaboration with Lévy Gorvy, with an exhibition of key works by Japanese master, TSUYOSHI MAEKAWA.\n            <br>\n            <br>\n            The presentation will include a selection of paintings by the artist from the 1950's and 60's, with important loans from Axel Vervoordt Gallery, Antwerp.\n            <br>\n            <br>\n            Tsuyoshi Maekawa (b. 1936) was a member of the Gutai Art Association, Japan's most significant avant-garde collective of the post-war era founded in 1954.\n\n            <a href=\"http://www.saatchigallery.com/art/tsuyoshi_maekawa.php\">Read more...</a>\n\n style=\"margin-top:11px; margin-left:15px;\">\n            </div>\n\n        </div>\n        <div class=\"clearfix\"></div>\n    </div>\n</div><div class=\"splitter\"></div><div <h3>EXHIBITIONISM: THE ROLLING STONES</h3>\n            </a>\n            <span class=\"date0height\">\n                    5 April - 4 September 2016\n                <!--<a  <span style=\"color: #cc0000;\">Click for tickets</span>\n                </a>-->\n            </span>\n            <div class=\"exmenu\">\n                <a href=\"http://www.saatchigallery.com/exhibition/reviews/exhibitionism_the_rolling_stones_35.htm\" id=\"review\" style=\"font-size:11px;\">Reviews of the exhibition</a>\n            </div>\n            <br>\n            <br>\n            Taking over the entire two floors of the Saatchi Gallery with 9 thematic galleries, <b>EXHIBITIONISM</b> combines over 500 original Stones' artefacts, with striking cinematic and interactive technologies offering the most comprehensive insight into the band's fascinating fifty year history.\n            <br>\n            <br>\n            From never before seen dressing room and backstage paraphernalia to rare instruments; original stage designs, iconic costumes, rare audio tracks and video footage; personal diaries; poster and album cover artwork; and unique wraparound cinematic experiences that celebrate every aspect of their Careers.\n            <br>\n            <br>\n            Centre stage is the musical heritage that took them from a London blues band in the early 1960s to inspirational cultural icons.\n            &nbsp;<a href=\"http://www.saatchigallery.com/art/rolling_stones.php\" class=\"moreinfo\">read more...</a>\n        </div>\n src=\"/smart-includes/assets/images/teamLab_image.jpg\" alt=\"In Our Paradise\"></div>\n        <div class=\"partshowbox_l\">\n            <a style=\"font-size: 1.2em;\">\n                <h3>teamLab:\n                    <br>\n                    Flutter of Butterflies Beyond Borders</h3>\n            </a>\n            <span class=\"date0height\">15 - 17 September 2015</span>\n            <div class=\"exmenu\"></div>\n            <br>\n            <br>\n            An immersive environment created by Japanese collective teamLab which consists of interactive projections rendered in real time. Reacting to the viewer's behaviour and movement, butterflies flutter across the room and an entire season of flowers blossom and wither away, exploring the cycle of birth and death. The installation featured as part of this year's START art fair's curated projects, received overwhelming attention from press and visitors and as a result will be open to public free of charge.\t class=\"picholder_r\">\n            <a href=\"http://www.saatchigallery.com/art/patek_philippe_2015.php\">\n                <img src=\"/smart-includes/assets/images/patek_philippe.jpg\" alt=\"Patek href=\"http://www.saatchigallery.com/art/patek_philippe_2015.php\" class=\"titlefont\">\n                <h3>Patek Philippe Watch Art Grand Exhibition</h3>\n            </a><span class=\"date0height\">27 May - 7 June 2015 </span>\n            <br>\n            <br>\n            <span class=\"date0height\">Monday - Friday: 09:00 to 19:00<br>\n                Saturday 6th June: 09:00 to 20:00 - last admission at 19:00<br>\n                Sunday 7th June: 09:00 to 16:00  - last admission at 15:30\n            </span>\n            <br>\n            <br>\n            <br>\n            <div class=\"exmenu\"></div>\n            <br>\n            <br>\n            This unique exhibition offers a rare insider's perspective into the art of watchmaking within a family company. \n            <br>\n            <br>\n            Visitors will explore over 400 exhibits, presented across 15 themed rooms. Occupying over 2000 m² these areas will recreate the world of Patek Philippe from the company's historic Geneva headquarters to its workshop and museum. Artisans will be on hand to demonstrate their unique rare handcrafts such as enamelling, guilloche work and precious stone setting. \n            <br>\n            <br>\n            'Watch Art' is designed as a captivating interactive exhibition which will ignite your passion for artisanship and deepen your knowledge of fine watchmaking. &nbsp;&nbsp;  <a href=\"/art/patek_philippe_2015.php\" class=\"moreinfo\">read more...</a>\n        </div>\n    </div>\n    <div class=\"clearfix\"></div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"splitter\"></div><div class=\"exhibition\">\n    <div class=\"exdescription\">\n        <div class=\"picholder_r\">\n            <a href=\"http://www.hermes.com/wanderland\" target=\"_blank\">\n                <img src=\"/smart-includes/assets/images/hermes_wanderland.jpg\" border=\"0\"></a>\n            <br>\n            <br>\n        </div>\n        <div class=\"partshowbox_l\">\n            <a href=\"http://www.saatchigallery.com/art/hermes_wanderland.php\" class=\"titlefont\">\n                <h3>Hermès Wanderland</h3>\n            </a>\n            <span class=\"date0height\">Starts on 9 April - Ends on 2 May 2015 at 01:00pm</span>\n            <br>\n            <br>\n            This exhibition shines a light on Hermès, the iconic French house. Inspired by ‘flanerie’, the art of urban wandering, each room presents a series of installations in various media, created by a diverse selection of artists. From the Parisian square, to the covered passage, or a cafe of forgotten objects this veritable extended cabinet of curiosities will delight and intrigue visitors, inviting them to be enveloped by the colour, sounds and images that surround them.  &nbsp;<a href=\"/art/hermes_wanderland.php\" class=\"moreinfo\">read more...</a>\n            <br>\n            <br>\n            <table border=\"0\">\n 9 Sept 2014</span>\n    <div class=\"exmenu\">\n        <a href=\"http://www.saatchigallery.com/exhibition/installation_views/abstract_america_today_8.htm\" id=\"preview\">Installation Views</a>\n        <a href=\"http://www.saatchigallery.com/exhibition/reviews/abstract_america_today_8.htm\" id=\"review\">Reviews of the exhibition</a>\n    </div>\n    <div class=\"exdescription\">\n        <div class=\"picholder\">\n            <img src=\"/smart-includes/assets/images/abstract_america_today.jpg\" alt=\"Abstract America Today\">\n        </div>\n        <div class=\"authorlinks\"><a href=\"/artists/lisa_anne_auerbach_abstract_america_today.htm\">Lisa Anne Auerbach</a><a href=\"/artists/trudy_benson_abstract_america_today.htm\">Trudy Benson</a><a href=\"/artists/paul_bloodgood_abstract_america_today.htm\">Paul Bloodgood</a><a href=\"/artists/keltie_ferris_abstract_america_today.htm\">Keltie Ferris</a><a href=\"/artists/wyatt_kahn_abstract_america_today.htm\">Wyatt Kahn</a><a href=\"/artists/ivan_morley_abstract_america_today.htm\">Ivan Morley</a><a href=\"/artists/jackie_saccoccio_abstract_america_today.htm\">Jackie Saccoccio</a><a href=\"/artists/brent_wadden_abstract_america_today.htm\">Brent Wadden</a><a href=\"/artists/cullen_washington_jr_abstract_america_today.htm\">Cullen Washington Jr</a></div>\n        <br clear=\"all\">\n    </div>\n    <div class=\"exnotice\"></div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"splitter\"></div><div class=\"exhibition\">\n    <div class=\"exdescription\">\n        <div class=\"picholder_r\">\n            <a href=\"http://www.saatchigallery.com/mpp/\">\n                <img src=\"/smart-includes/assets/images/mpp_11.jpg\" alt=\"Motion Photography Prize\"></a>\n        </div>\n        <div class=\"partshowbox_l\">\n            <a href=\"http://www.saatchigallery.com/mpp/\" class=\"titlefont\">\n                <h3>Motion Photography Prize</h3>\n            </a><span class=\"date0height\">17 April - 25 May 2014</span>\n            <!--<div class=\"exmenu\"> <a id=\"review\" href=\"http://www.saatchigallery.com/art/red_never_follows_reviews.php\" style=\"font-size:1.2em;\">Reviews of the exhibition</a> </div>-->\n            <br>\n            <br>\n            The first global open entry competition for artists and creative people working with animated GIFs. class=\"partshowbox_l\">\n            <a href=\"http://www.saatchigallery.com/art/hong_kong_eye.htm\" class=\"titlefont\">\n                <h3>Hong Kong Eye 2012</h3>\n            </a>\n            <span class=\"date0height\">5 December 2012 - 12 January 2013</span>\n            <div class=\"exmenu\"><a id=\"review\" href=\"http://www.saatchigallery.com/exhibition/reviews/hong_kong_eye_2012_16.htm\" style=\"font-size: 1.2em;\">Reviews of the exhibition</a> </div>\n            <br>\n            <br>\n    <div class=\"exnotice1\" style=\"width: 260px; float: left; font-size: 11px; clear: none !important\">\n                <b>PRESENTED BY:</b><br>\n                <img src=\"/smart-includes/assets/images/prudential_logo.jpg\">\n            </div>\n        </div>\n    </div>\n    <div class=\"clearfix\"></div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"splitter\"></div><div class=\"exhibition\">\n    <div class=\"exdescription\">\n        <div class=\"picholder_r\">\n            <a href=\"http://www.saatchigallery.com/art/the_little_black_jacket.php\">\n                <img src=\"/smart-includes/assets/images/the_little_black_jacket_chanel.jpg\" border=\"0\"></a>\n            <br>\n            <br>\n        </div>\n        <div class=\"partshowbox_l\">\n            <a href=\"http://www.saatchigallery.com/art/the_little_black_jacket.php\" class=\"titlefont\">\n                <h3>The Little Black Jacket</h3>\n            </a>\n            <span class=\"date0height\">12 October - 4 November 2012</span>\n            <br>\n            <br>\n            CHANEL's photographic exhibition dedicated to Karl Lagerfeld's latest book, 'The Little Black Jacket: CHANEL's classic revisited by Karl Lagerfeld and Carine Roitfeld', will open at the Saatchi Gallery in London in October.\n            <br>\n            <br>\n            The public will discover the versatility and timelessness of the iconic CHANEL jacket through Karl Lagerfeld's 113 photographs, modelled on a range of friends of the House, with each personality adapting the garment to reflect their own inimitable style - worn as a cape on singer Lily Allen, draped around model Stella Tennant, or even transformed into a vest on model Edie Campbell.\n&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href=\"http://www.saatchigallery.com/art/the_little_black_jacket.php\" class=\"moreinfo\">read more...</a>\n        </div>\n        <div class=\"exnotice\">\n            <b>PRESENTED BY:</b>\n font-weight: bold;\">PROJECT ROOMS</div>\n    <a href=\"http://www.saatchigallery.com/artists/jon_rafman.htm\" class=\"underliner\">\n        <h3>JON RAFMAN</h3>\n    </a>\n    <span class=\"date\">26 July - 4 November 2012</span>\n    <div class=\"exmenu\">\n        <a href=\"http://www.saatchigallery.com/exhibition/reviews/jon_rafman_18.htm\" id=\"review\">Reviews of the exhibition</a>\n        <a id=\"preview\" href=\"http://www.saatchigallery.com/exhibition/installation_views/jon_rafman_26.htm\">Installation Views</a>\n    </div>\n    <div class=\"exdescription\">\n        <div class=\"picholder\">\n            <a href=\"http://www.saatchigallery.com/artists/jon_rafman.htm\">\n                <img src=\"/smart-includes/assets/images/Rv888-Finnmark-Norway-2010.jpg\" border=\"0\" alt=\"Jon Rafman\"></a>\n        </div>\n        <div class=\"authorlinks1\">\n            <b>The Nine Eyes of Google Street View</b><br>\n            <br>\n            A year after Google Street View was launched, Montreal-based artist Jon Rafman started collecting screen captures from the site - accidents and incidents never intended for public consumption, as well as moments reminiscent of the photographic styles of real photographers. The result is his ongoing series <i>The Nine Eyes of Google Street View</i>, part of which has been shown for the first time in the UK at the Saatchi Gallery.\n            <br>\n            <br>\n        </div>\n    </div>\n    <div class=\"clearfix\"></div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"splitter\"></div><div class=\"exhibition\">\n    <!--<div style=\"font-size:11px;\">Previous exhibition</div>-->\n    <a href=\"http://www.saatchigallery.com/art/the-art-of-chess.htm\" class=\"underliner\">\n        <h3>THE ART OF CHESS</h3>\n    </a>\n    <span class=\"date\">8 September - 3 October 2012</span>\n    <div class=\"exmenu\">\n        <a href=\"http://www.saatchigallery.com/exhibition/reviews/the_art_of_chess_19.htm\" id=\"review\">Reviews of the exhibition</a>\n    </div>\n    <div class=\"exdescription\">\n        <div class=\"picholder\">\n            <a href=\"http://www.saatchigallery.com/art/the-art-of-chess.htm\">\n                <img src=\"/smart-includes/assets/images/the-art-of-chess_sm_2.jpg\" border=\"0\" alt=\"THE ART OF CHESS\"></a>\n        </div>\n        <div class=\"authorlinks1\">\n            This collaboration with RS&amp;A and Hugo Boss brings together 16 chess sets designed by some of the world's leading contemporary artists in celebration of the 'game of kings' and its continued relevance to the creative arts. &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href=\"http://www.saatchi-gallery.co.uk/current/the-art-of-chess.htm\" class=\"moreinfo\">read more...</a>\n            <br>\n            <br>\n            In association with :\n            <br>\n            <a href=\"http://www.hugoboss.com/\" target=\"_blank\">\n                <img src=\"/smart-includes/assets/images/boss_logo_sm.jpg\" border=\"0\"></a>\n            <br>\n            <br>\n        </div>\n    </div>\n    <div class=\"clearfix\"></div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"splitter\"></div><div class=\"exhibition\">\n    <div class=\"exdescription\">\n        <div class=\"picholder_r\"><a href=\"http://www.saatchigallery.com/art/korean_eye.htm\">\n            <img src=\"/smart-includes/assets/images/ke_image.jpg\" alt=\"Korean Eye\"></a></div>\n        <div class=\"partshowbox_l\">\n            <a href=\"http://www.saatchigallery.com/art/korean_eye.htm\" class=\"titlefont\">\n                <h3>Korean Eye 2012</h3>\n            </a><span class=\"date0height\">26 July - Made from papier mâché, Ryman's giant man reclines in a dreamy world, somewhere between Sunday morning lie-in bliss and nervous breakdown, basking in the clutter of notebooks, beer cans and open bags of crisps.\n            <br>\n            <br>\n        </div>\n    </div>\n    <div class=\"clearfix\"></div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"splitter\"></div><div class=\"exhibition\">\n    <div style=\"font-size: 11px; font-weight: bold;\">PROJECT ROOM</div>\n    <a href=\"http://www.saatchigallery.com/project_room/emily_prince.htm\" class=\"underliner\">\n        <h3>EMILY PRINCE</h3>\n    </a>\n    <span class=\"date\">7th January - 7th May 2010</span>\n    <div class=\"exmenu\">\n        <a href=\"http://www.saatchigallery.com/exhibition/reviews/emily_prince.htm\" id=\"review\">Reviews of the exhibition</a>\n    </div>\n    <div class=\"exdescription\">\n        <div class=\"picholder\">\n            <a href=\"http://www.saatchigallery.com/project_room/emily_prince.htm\">\n                <img src=\"/smart-includes/assets/images/emily_prince_sm.jpg\" border=\"0\" alt=\"Emily Prince\"></a>\n        </div>\n        <div class=\"authorlinks1\">\n            <b>American Servicemen and Women Who Have Died in Iraq and Afghanistan (but not Including the Wounded, nor the Iraqis nor the Afghans)</b>\n            <br>\n            <br>\n            A tribute to every American soldier killed in Iraq and Afghanistan since 2004. Comprising of 5,158 drawings - one for every fallen soldier to date. Rendered in graphite pencil, each portrait appears on small coloured cards which correspond to the skin tone of soldiers.\n        </div>\n    </div>\n    <div class=\"clearfix\"></div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"splitter\"></div><div class=\"exhibition\">\n    <div style=\"font-size: 11px; font-weight: bold;\">PROJECT ROOM</div>\n    <a href=\"http://www.saatchigallery.com/project_room/aleksandra_mir.htm\" class=\"underliner\">\n        <h3>ALEKSANDRA MIR</h3>\n    </a>\n    <span class=\"date\">9th October 2008 - 4th January 2009</span>\n    <div class=\"exmenu\">\n        &nbsp;&nbsp;\n        <!--<a href=\"http://www.saatchigallery.com/project_room/aleksandra_mir_reviews.htm\"  id=\"review\">Reviews of the exhibition</a>-->\n    </div>\n    <div class=\"exdescription\">\n        <div class=\"picholder\">\n            <a href=\"http://www.saatchigallery.com/project_room/aleksandra_mir.htm\">\n                <img src=\"/smart-includes/assets/images/alexandra_mir_sm.jpg\" border=\"0\" alt=\"ALEXANDRA MIR\"></a>\n        </div>\n        <div class=\"authorlinks1\">\n            <br>\n            <b>Newsroom</b>\n            <br>\n            <br>\n            \"News becomes history as soon as it is reported. What fascinates me in talking about history is the paradoxical movement backwards while obviously propelling ahead with a story into the future. The 15-year time period covered in the show is of a recent past, a past that still unites many New Yorkers in recognition of a city at once familiar and long gone. \"\n            <br>\n
